  <script type="text/javascript">
   function blockScript( script ) {
    script.type = 'javascript/blocked';
    script.parentElement.removeChild( script );
    window.blockedAssets.push( script.src );

    /* ----- Makes it work on firefox ----- */
    var beforeScriptExecuteListener = function ( event ) {
      if ( script.getAttribute( 'type' ) === 'javascript/blocked' ) {
        event.preventDefault();
      }
      script.removeEventListener( 'beforescriptexecute', beforeScriptExecuteListener );
    }

    script.addEventListener( 'beforescriptexecute', beforeScriptExecuteListener );
  }

  function blockStylesheet( stylesheet ) {
    stylesheet.type = 'css/blocked';
    stylesheet.parentElement.removeChild( stylesheet );
    window.blockedAssets.push( stylesheet.href );
  }

  function blockUniversalAssets() {
    var ua = window.navigator.userAgent;
    var isMS = ( ua.indexOf('Trident/') > -1 || ua.indexOf('Edge/') > -1 );

    if ( isMS ) return;
    if ( !window.UNIVERSAL_BLOCKED_PATHS ) return;
    if ( !window.UNIVERSAL_BLOCKED_PATHS.includes( window.location.pathname )) return;

    window.blockedAssets = [];

    try {
      var assetObserver = new MutationObserver( function( mutations ) {
        if ( !window.UNIVERSAL_BLOCKED_PATHS ) return;
        if ( !window.UNIVERSAL_BLOCKED_PATHS.includes( window.location.pathname )) return;

        mutations.forEach( function( mutation ) {
          for ( var i = 0; i < mutation.addedNodes.length; i++ ) {
            var node = mutation.addedNodes[i];

            // Handle scripts
            if ( node.nodeType === 1 && node.tagName === 'SCRIPT' ) {
              var src = node.src || '';

              // Universal scripts
              if ( src.indexOf( '//assets.squarespace.com/universal/' ) > -1 ) {
                blockScript( node );
              }
            }

            // Handle stylesheets
            else if ( node.nodeType === 1 && node.tagName === 'LINK' ) {
              var href = node.href || '';

              // Universal stylesheets
              if ( href.indexOf( '//assets.squarespace.com/universal/' ) > -1 ) {
                blockStylesheet( node );
              } else if ( href.indexOf( '//static1.squarespace.com/static/sitecss/' ) > -1 ) {
                blockStylesheet( node );
              }
            }

          }
        })
      })

      assetObserver.observe( document.head, {
        childList: true,
        subtree: true,
      });
    }
    catch( exception ) {}
  }

  window.UNIVERSAL_BLOCKED_PATHS = [
    '/',
    '/mobile',
    '/ecommerce-website',
    '/website-design',
    '/website-marketing',
    '/ecommerce-website-tour',
    '/website-design-tour',
    '/website-marketing-tour',
    '/small-business-website',
    '/tour/photography-websites',
    '/tour/create-a-blog',
    '/tour/portfolio-website',
    '/tour/restaurant-websites',
    '/tour/music-website',
    '/tour/wedding-website',
    '/how-to-build-website',
    '/how-to-connect-a-domain',
    '/email-marketing',
    '/professional-email'
  ];
  blockUniversalAssets();
  </script>

        <div class="faq-feature-text__faqs" data-reveal-self="">
         <div class="faq-feature-text__faq" style="--reveal-delay: calc(1 * 0.05s + 0.2s);">
          <div class="faq-feature-text__faq-heading">
           <h3 tabindex="0">
            What does a Squarespace subscription include?
           </h3>
           <button aria-label="Open frequently asked question" class="faq-feature-text__faq-button" tabindex="0">
           </button>
          </div>
          <div class="faq-feature-text__answer-container">
           <div class="faq-feature-text__answer" tabindex="0">
            <p>
             Squarespace is an all-in-one content management system, or CMS. With a single subscription, you can create a website, host your content, register your own custom domain name, sell products, track your site’s analytics, and much more.
            </p>
            <p>
             Start with any template to create pages and organize your site, then customize it to match your own style.
            </p>
            <p>
             For a full list of features, visit our
             <a href="https://www.squarespace.com/feature-index/">
              feature index
             </a>
             and explore the Help Center for guides on Squarespace's many features.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="faq-feature-text__faq" style="--reveal-delay: calc(2 * 0.05s + 0.2s);">
          <div class="faq-feature-text__faq-heading">
           <h3 tabindex="0">
            Is Squarespace right for me?
           </h3>
           <button aria-label="Open frequently asked question" class="faq-feature-text__faq-button" tabindex="0">
           </button>
          </div>
          <div class="faq-feature-text__answer-container">
           <div class="faq-feature-text__answer" tabindex="0">
            <p>
             Everyone has unique needs for their website, so there’s one way to know if Squarespace is right for you: try it!
            </p>
            <p>
             We offer a free 14-day trial so you can explore our platform, begin building a site, and decide if you're ready to subscribe to Squarespace. If you're still not sure or if you need more time, you can extend it or start again later.
             <a href="https://support.squarespace.com/hc/articles/206536827" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
              Learn more about trials
             </a>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             For a visual preview before signing up, or to make the most of your trial, we recommend these resources:
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              Watch short
              <a href="https://support.squarespace.com/hc/categories/200204575-Videos" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
               Help videos
              </a>
              .
             </li>
             <li>
              Sign up for a live expert-led
              <a href="https://learning.squarespace.com/webinars" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
               webinar
              </a>
              .
             </li>
             <li>
              Explore at your own pace using the guides in this Help Center.
             </li>
            </ol>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="faq-feature-text__faq" style="--reveal-delay: calc(3 * 0.05s + 0.2s);">
          <div class="faq-feature-text__faq-heading">
           <h3 tabindex="0">
            Can I move to Squarespace from another platform?
           </h3>
           <button aria-label="Open frequently asked question" class="faq-feature-text__faq-button" tabindex="0">
           </button>
          </div>
          <div class="faq-feature-text__answer-container">
           <div class="faq-feature-text__answer" tabindex="0">
            <p>
             Absolutely. If you already own your domain or have a site hosted by another provider, you can move to Squarespace using these options:
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              If you already own a domain - You can
              <a href="https://support.squarespace.com/hc/articles/206542037" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
               transfer your domain to Squarespace
              </a>
              .
             </li>
             <li>
              If you already have a website - If you have a site with WordPress, Blogger, or Tumblr, you can import your blog content to Squarespace.
             </li>
             <li>
              If you already have an online store - If you have an online store with Shopify, Big Cartel, or Etsy, or can prepare
              <a href="https://support.squarespace.com/hc/articles/115000378108" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
               a list of products in a .csv
              </a>
              , you can import your products to Squarespace, then build your site using our templates and tools.
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             Since moving between website platforms can affect how search engines view your site, we recommend following
             <a href="https://support.squarespace.com/hc/articles/206543797" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
              these best practices
             </a>
             to protect your search ranking during your transition.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="faq-feature-text__faq" style="--reveal-delay: calc(4 * 0.05s + 0.2s);">
          <div class="faq-feature-text__faq-heading">

             .

   function resetCanonical() {
    try {
      var canonicalTag = document.querySelector('link[rel=canonical]');
      canonicalTag.href = document.location.origin || canonicalTag.href;
    }
    catch(err) {
      console.log('Unable to reset canonical.');
    }
  }
  if (document.location.pathname === '/') {
    resetCanonical();
  }
